# Style Transfer

```{.python .input  n=72}
%matplotlib inline
import matplotlib as mpl
mpl.rcParams['figure.dpi']= 150
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

from mxnet import image

style_img = image.imread('img/style/starry_night.jpg')
content_img = image.imread('img/content/golden_gate.jpg')

plt.imshow(style_img.asnumpy())
plt.show()
plt.imshow(content_img.asnumpy())
plt.show()
```

```{.python .input  n=53}
from mxnet import nd
import mxnet as mx

rgb_mean = nd.array([0.485, 0.456, 0.406])
rgb_std = nd.array([0.229, 0.224, 0.225])

def preprocess(img, image_shape):
    img = image.imresize(img, *image_shape)
    img = (img.astype('float32')/255 - rgb_mean) / rgb_std
    return img.transpose((2,0,1)).expand_dims(axis=0)

def postprocess(img):
    img = img[0].as_in_context(rgb_std.context)
    return (img.transpose((1,2,0))*rgb_std + rgb_mean).clip(0,1)
```

## Model

Use VGG 19 Pretrained Model from Imagenet.

```{.python .input  n=54}
from mxnet.gluon.model_zoo import vision as models

pretrained_net = models.vgg19(pretrained=True)
pretrained_net
```

```{.python .input  n=55}
style_layers = [0,5,10,19,28]
content_layers = [25]
```

```{.python .input  n=57}
from mxnet.gluon import nn

def get_net(pretrained_net, content_layers, style_layers):
    net = nn.Sequential()
    for i in range(max(content_layers+style_layers)+1):
        net.add(pretrained_net.features[i])
    return net

net = get_net(pretrained_net, content_layers, style_layers)
```

```{.python .input  n=58}
def extract_features(x, content_layers, style_layers):
    contents = []
    styles = []
    for i in range(len(net)):
        x = net[i](x)
        if i in style_layers:
            styles.append(x)
        if i in content_layers:
            contents.append(x)
    return contents, styles
```

## Define loss functions

```{.python .input  n=59}
def content_loss(yhat, y):
    return (yhat-y).square().mean()
```

Use Gram Matrics for style match

```{.python .input  n=60}
def gram(x):
    c = x.shape[1]
    n = x.size / x.shape[1]
    y = x.reshape((c, int(n)))
    return nd.dot(y, y.T) / n

gram(nd.ones((1,3,4,4)))
```

```{.json .output n=60}
[
 {
  "data": {
   "text/plain": "\n[[ 1.  1.  1.]\n [ 1.  1.  1.]\n [ 1.  1.  1.]]\n<NDArray 3x3 @cpu(0)>"
  },
  "execution_count": 60,
  "metadata": {},
  "output_type": "execute_result"
 }
]
```

```{.python .input  n=61}
def style_loss(yhat, gram_y):
    return (gram(yhat) - gram_y).square().mean()
```

Total Variation Denoising(https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Total_variation_denoising
Assume $x_{i,j}$ represents a pixel $(i,j)$ï¼Œthe loss function will be as below to make neighbors similar

$$
\sum_{i,j} |x_{i,j} - x_{i+1,j}| + |x_{i,j} - x_{i,j+1}|
$$

```{.python .input  n=62}
def tv_loss(yhat):
    return 0.5*((yhat[:,:,1:,:] - yhat[:,:,:-1,:]).abs().mean() +
                (yhat[:,:,:,1:] - yhat[:,:,:,:-1]).abs().mean())
```

```{.python .input  n=63}
channels = [net[l].weight.shape[0] for l in style_layers]
print(channels)
# More weights on hidden layers closer to inputs
style_weights = [1e4/n**2 for n in channels]
print(style_weights)
content_weights = [1]
tv_weight = 10
```

```{.json .output n=63}
[
 {
  "name": "stdout",
  "output_type": "stream",
  "text": "[64, 128, 256, 512, 512]\n[2.44140625, 0.6103515625, 0.152587890625, 0.03814697265625, 0.03814697265625]\n"
 }
]
```

```{.python .input  n=64}
def sum_loss(loss, preds, truths, weights):
    return nd.add_n(*[w*loss(yhat, y) for w, yhat, y in zip(
        weights, preds, truths)])
```

## Train

```{.python .input  n=65}
def get_contents(image_shape):
    content_x = preprocess(content_img, image_shape).copyto(ctx)
    content_y, _ = extract_features(content_x, content_layers, style_layers)
    return content_x, content_y

def get_styles(image_shape):
    style_x = preprocess(style_img, image_shape).copyto(ctx)
    _, style_y = extract_features(style_x, content_layers, style_layers)
    style_y = [gram(y) for y in style_y]
    return style_x, style_y
```

```{.python .input  n=66}
from time import time
from mxnet import autograd

def train(x, max_epochs, lr, lr_decay_epoch=200):
    tic = time()
    for i in range(max_epochs):
        with autograd.record():
            content_py, style_py = extract_features(
                x, content_layers, style_layers)
            content_L  = sum_loss(
                content_loss, content_py, content_y, content_weights)
            style_L = sum_loss(
                style_loss, style_py, style_y, style_weights)
            tv_L = tv_weight * tv_loss(x)
            loss = style_L + content_L + tv_L

        loss.backward()
        x.grad[:] /= x.grad.abs().mean()+1e-8
        x[:] -= lr * x.grad
        # add sync to avoid large mem usage
        nd.waitall()

        if i and i % 20 == 0:
            print('batch %3d, content %.2f, style %.2f, '
                  'TV %.2f, time %.1f sec' % (
                i, content_L.asscalar(), style_L.asscalar(),
                tv_L.asscalar(), time()-tic))
            tic = time()

        if i and i % lr_decay_epoch == 0:
            lr *= 0.1
            print('change lr to ', lr)

    plt.imshow(postprocess(x).asnumpy())
    plt.show()
    return x
```

## Train on small size `300 x 200` image. 
Use content image or style image for initialization to improve convergencce.

```{.python .input  n=67}
import sys
sys.path.append('..')
#import utils

image_shape = (300,200)

#ctx = utils.try_gpu()
ctx = mx.gpu()
net.collect_params().reset_ctx(ctx)

content_x, content_y = get_contents(image_shape)
style_x, style_y = get_styles(image_shape)

x = content_x.copyto(ctx)
x.attach_grad()

y = train(x, 500, 0.1)
```


## Train on large image.
Use the image trained above for initialization to improve convergence time

```{.python .input  n=70}
image_shape = (content_img.shape[1], content_img.shape[0])

content_x, content_y = get_contents(image_shape)
style_x, style_y = get_styles(image_shape)

x = preprocess(postprocess(y)*255, image_shape).copyto(ctx)
x.attach_grad()

z = train(x, 300, 0.1, 100)
```

## Save image

```{.python .input  n=69}
plt.imsave('result.png', postprocess(z).asnumpy())
```
